    doctor_address character varying(500) NOT NULL,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    updated_by integer NOT NULL,
    updated_date timestamp without time zone DEFAULT (now())::timestamp(0) without time zone NOT NULL,
    added_by integer NOT NULL,
    added_date timestamp without time zone DEFAULT (now())::timestamp(0) without time zone NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL
);




CREATE TABLE  pharmacy.t_temp_patient_registration (id serial NOT NULL,
    organization_id integer NOT NULL,
    unit_id integer NOT NULL,
    temp_uhid character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    patient_name character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    address character varying(500) NOT NULL,
    age integer NOT NULL,
    gender_id integer NOT NULL,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    updated_by integer NOT NULL,
    updated_date timestamp without time zone DEFAULT (now())::timestamp(0) without time zone NOT NULL,
    added_by integer NOT NULL,
    added_date timestamp without time zone DEFAULT (now())::timestamp(0) without time zone NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    prefix_id integer
);

CREATE TABLE pharmacy.t_return_of_empty_ampoules
(
	id serial NOT NULL,
	organization_id int NOT NULL,
	unit_id int NOT NULL,
	issue_id integer NOT NULL,
	patient_id integer NOT NULL,
	doctor_id integer NOT NULL,
	ward_id integer NOT NULL,
	bed_id integer NOT NULL,
	priority_id integer NOT NULL ,
	status_id integer NOT NULL,
	is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    updated_by integer NOT NULL,
    updated_date timestamp without time zone DEFAULT cast (now() as timestamp(0))  NOT NULL,
    added_by integer  NOT NULL,
    added_date timestamp without time zone DEFAULT cast (now() as timestamp(0))  NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pkey_return_of_empty_ampoules PRIMARY KEY (id),
    CONSTRAINT fkey_patient FOREIGN KEY (patient_id)
	REFERENCES patient.t_patient_registration (patient_id),
	CONSTRAINT fkey_doctor FOREIGN KEY (doctor_id)
     REFERENCES doctor.m_doctor_master (doctor_id),
	 CONSTRAINT fkey_status FOREIGN KEY (status_id)
     REFERENCES public.m_status (id),
	CONSTRAINT fkey_bed FOREIGN KEY (bed_id)
     REFERENCES adt.m_bed_master (bed_id),
	CONSTRAINT fkey_ward FOREIGN KEY (ward_id)
     REFERENCES adt.m_ward_master (ward_id),
	 CONSTRAINT fkey_issue FOREIGN KEY (issue_id)
     REFERENCES pharmacy.t_issue (id),
	CONSTRAINT fkey_priority FOREIGN KEY (priority_id)
     REFERENCES adt.m_priority_master (priority_id),
	   CONSTRAINT at_added_by FOREIGN KEY (added_by)
		REFERENCES public.m_user_master (user_id),
		CONSTRAINT at_updated_by FOREIGN KEY (updated_by)
		REFERENCES public.m_user_master (user_id),
		CONSTRAINT at_organisation FOREIGN KEY (organization_id)
		REFERENCES public.m_organization_master (organization_id),
		CONSTRAINT at_unit FOREIGN KEY (unit_id)
		REFERENCES public.m_unit_master (unit_id)
);
